<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взаимный.html>взаи́мно</a> (19586)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взаимный.html>взаи́мный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzaímnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взаимный.html>взаи́мно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzaímno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>mutually</li>
<li>me too (e.g. I'm glad to meet you too)</li>
<li>the same to you (the same wishes)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взаимный.html>взаи́мно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzaímno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взаимный.html>взаи́мный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzaímnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взаимный.html>взаи́мный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vzaímnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">-ость</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взаимность.html>взаи́мность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzaímnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взаимность.html>взаи́мности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взаимность.html>взаи́мности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взаимность.html>взаи́мностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>reciprocity, mutuality
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвечать.html>отвеча́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:взаимность.html>взаи́мностью</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otvečátʹ <b>vzaímnostʹju</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reciprocate / return somebody's feelings / love / affection</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взаимодействие.html>взаимоде́йствие</a> (6255)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">взаимо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzaimo-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mutual, co-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:действие.html>де́йствие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">déjstvije</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">action, acting</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zusammenwirkung</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wechselwirkung</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взаимодействие.html>взаимоде́йствие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzaimodéjstvije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взаимодействие.html>взаимоде́йствия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взаимодействие.html>взаимоде́йствия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взаимодействие.html>взаимоде́йствий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>interaction, interplay
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:создание.html>созда́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:доброжелательный.html>доброжела́тельной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:атмосфера.html>атмосфе́ры</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:взаимодействие.html>взаимоде́йствии</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:учащийся.html>уча́щихся</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sozdánije dobroželátelʹnoj atmosféry pri <b>vzaimodéjstvii</b> učáščixsja</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the creation of a friendly atmosphere for student <b>interaction</b></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>cooperation, coordination
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взаимодействие.html>взаимоде́йствие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:региональный.html>региона́льных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:столичный.html>столи́чных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:компания.html>компа́ний</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzaimodéjstvije</b> regionálʹnyx i stolíčnyx kompánij</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the <b>cooperation</b> between regional and metropolitan companies</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взбегать.html>взбега́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzbegátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взбежать.html>взбежа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run up <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to run in an upward direction, e.g. up a hill</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взбежать.html>взбежа́ть</a> (16018)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взбежать.html>взбежа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzbežátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взбегать.html>взбега́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run up <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to run in an upward direction, e.g. up a hill</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взбесить.html>взбеси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzbesítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взбеситься.html>взбеси́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzbesítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беситься.html>беси́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become rabid</li>

***взбить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взбить.html>взбить</a> (14569)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взбить.html>взби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzbítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взбивать.html>взбива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to beat up, to fluff, to whip, to whisk (e.g. cream)</li></ol>
